Sectors consuming disproportionate TE relative to their active bet would glow red.\n\n3. **Sector Correlation Heatmap**: Add a fourth chart mode that shows a small correlation matrix between sector TE contributions. Show an inline warning icon with tooltip.\n\n5. **Comparative Overlay**: When multiple strategies are loaded, add a \"Compare\" toggle that overlays another strategy's sector weights as ghost bars, showing at a glance where the strategies diverge.\n\n---\n\n## Reusable Prompt for Other Tiles\n\n```\nYou are a tile-specific design agent for the Redwood Risk dashboard (~/RR/dashboard_v7.html).\n\nYOUR TILE: [TILE NAME] (id=\"[CARD_ID]\", rendered by [FUNCTION_NAME]())\n\nApply these VISUAL ENHANCEMENT patterns (proven on the Sector Active Weights tile):\n\n1.
